Just dial 0 in the room and the response will be prompt.

The hotel employs many Southeast Asian employees, and it suddenly gives the illusion of a Southeast Asian vacation. The entire park is huge, and you have to take a shuttle bus to get everywhere. If it doesn't rain, it's not a long walk.

The room is large, compatible with both Chinese simplicity and Western simplicity and modernity. The curtains will automatically open when you enter the door, truly facing the sea with spring flowers blooming. Even if you have a garden view room, you can see a little bit of the sea if you live on the 3rd floor. The breakfast buffet was rich, but because it was humid and rainy at the beach, the bread always felt soft.

I would like to commend Edison at the front desk. When we checked in very late, he was still very patient and took out a map to explain. Called the front desk to ask someone to pick us up, made three phone calls, and waited for at least 20 minutes (during the period, there was a battery car that told us to wait at the same place due to different directions), and finally ushered in a battery car specially for picking us up. Even if the unlucky hotel resen**ent is forged. Because the hotel's Chinese restaurant is so popular, I didn't want to wait for an hour and didn't have any choices, so I ordered takeaway, which was delivered in about an hour. After eating at night, I'm afraid there will be a smell in the room, just like room 2311 next door, I put the takeaway garbage outside the room. (emphasis added)
12.25 In the morning, I ordered some simple room breakfast, and after eating, I set off for the day's itinerary. After a day of playing, I went back to the hotel to rest (after 5:00 pm), and found that the garbage we placed at the gate of 2313 last night was still in place, and the garbage at the gate of 2311 had been collected. At that time, I had a bad feeling in my heart. As soon as I entered the room, sure enough, the room had not been cleaned, the breakfast plate was still there, and the room smelled of leftovers and pickles.
At that time, I first called to reflect that I wanted to change the room. Later, when I thought it was my family and I who wanted to change the room, I went out to the bar to clean up my mood. The cleaning staff also came to clean the room within half an hour. We did accidentally turn on Do Not Disturb in our room, so the cleaning aunt said that in this case, she really didn't dare to enter the door. I understand, but this statement was overturned the next day, because I reflected this situation when I checked out. The hotel said that if the guest‚Äôs do not disturb light is on, the hotel will call/contact the guest to confirm whether to clean the room. We did not receive a call . And there is also garbage at the door, why is the garbage in 2311 next door taken away, and our garbage in 2313 is still at the door? ? ? ? ? ? ? Can't the garbage outside the house be taken away without entering the door? ? ? ? ? incomprehensible.
Check out at noon on 12.26, ushered in a speechless and angry climax. We first called to ask if we need to check out in the lobby. After confirming the settlement and deducting the fee, we can choose to give the room card to the brother in the battery car, or leave the room card in the room and leave. After confirming with the front desk on the phone, we agreed that please send a car to pick us up, and we will go directly to the parking lot. The trolley guy came soon. There was another anxious guest in the same car. The tram guy quickly took us to the lobby without asking/confirming. We hurriedly said, we don‚Äôt go to the lobby, this is our room card . The tram man said: "Then you didn't say it earlier." excuse me? ? ? ? ? I said you didn't ask, and I communicated with the front desk and I went directly to the parking lot. I didn't know that you came to the lobby to see us off, and I didn't know if the passenger in the same car wanted to go to the lobby.
He sent us to the parking lot without a word, unloaded the two big luggage, because we were facing inward from the rear of the car, the tram man said: Move your car forward to put the luggage. We thought he would come to help us pack our luggage after moving the car, but in the end, this grandson drove away in a battery car? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? Leave us three girls in the parking lot. . . .
At that time, I got angry and called the front desk, asking the same tram man to come back to carry the luggage and apologize. The front desk should have said in the company‚Äôs WeChat group that there are customers who are parking and need to carry their luggage. During the waiting process, two very enthusiastic and friendly tram boys passed by and asked to help us carry our luggage. I politely refused and asked for that rude tram man. Come back to carry luggage and apologize.
After waiting for a while, the tram guy came back, unapologetic, and kept saying he was too busy just now. After unloading the luggage, he turned his back and said to us that my name is Hanks, and you can complain about me. I was completely speechless: okay, you are bigger than me, you don't care about complaints at all, I understand.

In fact, I might not be so angry if any of these three incidents happened, and I am too lazy to write bad reviews and post them on any social platforms. But the successive episodes made me unable to shut up and swallow my anger. I chose to share my experience with everyone to help everyone avoid lightning.
